----

Original blurb:

Romance. Intrigue. Domination. Control. Subservience. Clarity. Epiphany. Release. EUPHORIA. None of these words relate to the contents of this book in any way whatsoever.

Sometimes in life we reach an impasse. A void in our being so profound that we feel unable to overcome it, as if merely acknowledging its existence will stifle our progress towards true happiness. And sometimes we forget how to write the phrase "Shades of grey." This book provides arguably the finest solution to the latter problem by repeating the phrase fifty-thousand times. Simply open the book to any page and - voila! - you will find one hundred and seventy-two examples.

If you glue this book to your hand, you will be unable to put it down.

----

"Fifty Thousand Shades of Grey" by S. C. Ashen.

All rights reserved.
